08/04/2024, 17:12 - Harsh Singh: Important Notice Regarding Scholarship Disbursement

Dear Students,
We wanted to address a matter concerning the disbursement of scholarships for certain branches of study at our institute. It has come to our attention that, unfortunately, there has been a delay in the processing of scholarships for some of our students.

The scholarship granting authority (Samaj Kalyan) has indicated that the delay is caused by a failure to lock the necessary data from our institute.

We want to assure you that the data was locked for all branches at institute level. Furthermore, we take this matter very seriously. We are in constant communication with the relevant authorities and the NIC to expedite the process.

Thank you for your patience and understanding.
DSW, IET Lucknow
